  <script>
   Sentry.onLoad(function() {
      var sentryBeforeSend = function(event, hint) {
        var errorMsg = hint.originalException ?
          hint.originalException.message : '';

        // `document.createEvent()` called with an incorrect context.
        if (/^Illegal invocation/.test(errorMsg)) {
          try {
            document.createEvent('FooCustomEvent');
          } catch {
            return null;
          }
        }
        // common videojs error
        if (/AbortError/i.test(errorMsg) && window.videojs !== undefined) {
          return null;
        }
        return event;
      }
      var sentryEnvironment = 'production';
      Sentry.init({
        environment: sentryEnvironment,
        sampleRate: sentryEnvironment === 'production' ? 0.1 : 1,
        whitelistUrls: [/\.thedrive\.com/],
        ignoreErrors: [
          /ResizeObserver loop limit exceeded/,
          // Brightcove \(VideoJS\) error
          /The play\(\) request was interrupted by a call to pause\(\)/,
          /platform\.twitter\.com/,
          /youtube\.com/,
          /facebook\.com/,
          // prebid3.23.0.js bug
          /Cannot read property \'getSlotElementId\' of undefined/,
          /Blocked a frame with origin/,
          /Blocked a restricted frame with origin/
        ],
        beforeSend: sentryBeforeSend
    });
    });

  <script>
   /* Various reusable utilities and debugging tools - shared with BV Codebase */
var utils = {
    queryString: {},
    init: function() {
        // parse and store the query string on init
        var queryString = this.queryString;

        location.search.slice(1).split('&').forEach(function(pair) {
            pair = pair.split('=');
            queryString[pair[0]] = decodeURIComponent(pair[1] || '');
        });

        // log CLS to console if ?debug_cls=true
        if (queryString.debug_cls === 'true') {
            this.logLayoutShift();
        }
    },
    logLayoutShift: function() {
        var totalShift = 0;

        try {
            function perfObserver(list) {
                for (i = 0; i < list.getEntries().length; i++) {
                    var entry = list.getEntries()[i];

                    totalShift += entry.value;
                    console.log('Layout shift: ' + entry.value + '. CLS: ' + totalShift + '.');
                }
            }

            var po = new PerformanceObserver(perfObserver);

            po.observe({
                type: 'layout-shift',
                buffered: true
            });
        } catch (e) {
            console.log('PerformanceObserver not supported.');
        }
    },

    setCookie: function(cname, cvalue, exDays) {
        var d = new Date();
        var exTime = 2147483647;  // The maximum, can be overridden with exDays
        var expires;
        if (typeof exDays !== 'undefined') {
            d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exDays*24*60*60*1000));
            exTime = d.toUTCString();
        }
        expires = "expires=" + exTime;
        document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
    },

    getCookie: function(cname) {
        var v = document.cookie.match('(^|;) ?' + cname + '=([^;]*)(;|$)');
        return v ? v[2] : null;
    },

    deleteCookie: function(cname) {
        utils.setCookie(cname, '', -1);
    },

    /**
     * Load a script once.
     *
     * Use the id to ensure a script is only loaded once.
     *
     * @param d (object) The document object.
     * @param id (str) The id for the script tag.
     * @param src (str) The source for the script.
     * @param data (object) Data attributes for the script.
     * @param el (DOM Node) A DOM node to use to place the script tag. Defaults to using the head.
     * @param async (bool) True if you want to load the script async
     */
    loadScript: function(d, id, src, callback, data, el, async) {
        // Should use a unique ID so this doesn't collide and fail to load
        if (document.querySelector('#' + id)) {
            if (typeof callback === 'function') {
                callback();
            }
            return;
        }

        var script = d.createElement('script');
        script.src = src;
        script.id = id;
        if (typeof callback === 'function') {
            script.onload = callback;
        }

        if (data) {
            Object.entries(data).forEach(function(attr) {
                script.setAttribute(attr[0], attr[1]);
            });
        }

        el = el || d.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
        el.appendChild(script);
    }
};

utils.init();

window.BVTests = (function() {
    var tests = {};
    var userBuckets = {};
    var cookiePrefix = 'bv_test__';
    var debugParam = 'debug_bv_tests';
    var debugLogs = ('debug_tests' in utils.queryString);

    function _log() {
        if (!debugLogs) {
            return;
        }
        console.log.apply(console, arguments);
    }

    function sample(rate) {
        // Put rate inside our boundaries
        rate = Math.min(100, Math.max(0, rate));
        return rate > Math.floor(Math.random() * 100);
    }

    /**
     * Create a split test with a given name, bucket the user.
     *
     * @param name (str) The test name.
     * @param config (object) The test config.
     *
     * Config object contains bucket names and percentages. Control is not required and will
     * be ignored. Control will automatically get the leftover values.
     *
     * Example:
     *
     *   BVTests.create('someTest', {
     *     bucketA: 5
     *   });
     *
     * In the above example, we create a test called "someTest" where control is 95% and
     * bucketA is 5%;
     */
    function create(name, config) {
        if (tests[name]) {
            return;
        }

        // If we're using a query string, force a bucket even if the bucket doesn't exist yet
        // Debug param would be something like `debug_bv_tests=testName-testBucket,test2Name-testBucket`
        var qsTests = utils.queryString[debugParam];
        if (qsTests) {
            qsTests = qsTests.split(',');
            for (var i=0; i<qsTests.length; i++) {
                var _qsTest = qsTests[i].split('-');
                if (_qsTest.length === 2 && _qsTest[0] === name) {
                    userBuckets[name] = _qsTest[1];
                    utils.setCookie(cookiePrefix + name, _qsTest[1]);
                    _log('User bucketed from query string param:', name, _qsTest[1]);
                    return;
                }
            }
        }

        // If the user is already cookied with a valid bucket, use it
        var cookiedBucket = utils.getCookie(cookiePrefix + name);
        if (cookiedBucket && (cookiedBucket === 'control' || cookiedBucket in config)) {
            userBuckets[name] = cookiedBucket;
            _log('User bucketed from cookie:', name, cookiedBucket);
            return;
        }

        tests[name] = config;
        userBuckets[name] = 'control';  // Default to control

        // Bucket the user
        for (var bucket in config) {
            // Skip control, we don't accept a control bucket
            if (bucket == 'control')  {
                continue;
            }

            var rate = parseInt(config[bucket]);

            // If bucket is chosen, assign user to the bucket
            if (sample(rate)) {
                _log('user sampled:', rate, name, bucket);
                userBuckets[name] = bucket;
                break;
            }
        }

        // Set the users bucket as a cookie
        utils.setCookie(cookiePrefix + name, userBuckets[name]);
        _log('user bucketed:', name, userBuckets[name]);
    }

    /**
     * Build the targeting string based on tests created.
     *
     * Example: testName-testBucket,test2Name-testBucket
     *
     * TODO: Add validation on name and value. Cannot contain '-' or ','.
     */
    function getTargetingValue() {
        var targeting = [];
        for (var name in userBuckets) {
            var value = userBuckets[name];
            targeting.push(name + '-' + value);
        }
        return targeting;
    }

    return {
        create: create,
        getValue: function(name) { return userBuckets[name]; },
        getUserBuckets: function() { return userBuckets; },
        getTargetingValue: getTargetingValue
    }
})();

(function() {

    /* Leaving this here as an example:
    // Ad delay test
    BVTests.create('bv_adDelay', {
      delay1: 50,
    });
    */

    BVTests.create('td_noSpotTD10', {
        enabled: 10,
    });
    BVTests.create('td_footerClose10', {
        enabled: 10,
    });
    BVTests.create('td_taboola10', {
        enabled: 10,
    });

    window.__adDelay = 0;

    window.AD_EXPERIENCE_GO = 'td_noSpotTD10-control';
    window.TABOOLA_EXPERIENCE = 'td_taboola10-control';

    /* Exclude The War Zone & Reviews from the enabled legs */
    if (
        window.location.href.match(/the-war-zone/) ||
        window.location.href.match(/reviews/) ||
        window.location.href.match(/car-insurance/) ||
        window.location.href.match(/car-warranty/)
    ) {
        window.AD_EXPERIENCE_GO = 'td_noSpotTD10-exclude';
        window.TABOOLA_EXPERIENCE = 'td_taboola10-exclude';
    } else {
        if ( BVTests.getValue('td_noSpotTD10') === 'enabled' ) {
            window.AD_EXPERIENCE_GO = 'td_noSpotTD10-enabled';
        }
        if ( BVTests.getValue('td_taboola10') === 'enabled' ) {
            window.TABOOLA_EXPERIENCE = 'td_taboola10-enabled';
        }
    }

    if ( BVTests.getValue('td_footerClose10') === 'enabled' ) {
        window.trackADMData = { closeButton: true };
    } else {
        window.trackADMData = { closeButton: false };
    }
})();

      googletag.pubads().setTargeting('tests', [window.TABOOLA_EXPERIENCE, window.AD_EXPERIENCE_GO, window.CLOSE_BUTTON_EXPERIENCE]);

      if ( window.location.href.match(/motorcycle/) ) {
        googletag.pubads().setTargeting('targeting_keyword', 'motorcycle');
      }
  });

  if (adParams.ptype === "main" && adParams.zone !== "homepage") {
    adParams.zone += "/main";
  }

  adSlotTargets.ptype = adParams.ptype;

    if ("homepage" === "homepage") {

    }
  }

  if ( ENABLE_GUMGUM_STICKY ) {
    window.feAdSlotsConfig['/21817035599/Desktop_Tablet_Sticky_Footer']['sizes'].push([1,1]);
    window.feAdSlotsConfig['/21817035599/Desktop_Tablet_Sticky_Footer']['pbjsBid_gumgum_params'] = {'sticky': '8fnrcefg'};

    window.feAdSlotsConfig['/21817035599/Mobile_Sticky_Footer']['sizes'].push([1,1]);
    window.feAdSlotsConfig['/21817035599/Mobile_Sticky_Footer']['pbjsBid_gumgum_params'] = {'sticky': '8fnrcefg'};
  }

  window.feAdConfig = {
    templateVars: {
      ads: {"pageType":"main"},
      tgx: {"ch":"homepage","zone":"homepage"},
      layoutName: 'homepage'
    },
    isMobile: window.innerWidth < 728,
    decideDefineAd: function(adSlotKey, slotObj) {
      var finish = function(defined, definedReason, definedCount) {
        slotObj.defined = defined;
        slotObj.definedReason = definedReason;
        slotObj.definedCount = definedCount;
        return slotObj;
      };
      if (!feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotKey]) {
        return finish(false, 'No such ad');
      }
      if (feAdConfig.isMobile && adSlotKey.indexOf('Mobile') === -1) {
        return finish(false, 'Ad is not for mobile');
      }
      if (!feAdConfig.isMobile && adSlotKey.indexOf('Mobile') !== -1) {
        return finish(false, 'Ad is only for mobile');
      }
      if (slotObj.global) {
        return finish(true, 'Ad is global');
      }
      if (!slotObj.shouldDefine) {
        return finish(false, 'Not global, no definition logic');
      }
      return finish.apply(null, slotObj.shouldDefine());
    },
    log: function() {
      var args = Array.from(arguments);
      args.unshift('FE AD |');
      console.log.apply(console, args);
    },
    warn: function() {
      var args = Array.from(arguments);
      args.unshift('FE AD |');
      console.warn.apply(console, args);
    }
  };

  var maybeDisplayFeAdSlot = function(divId) {
    var slotDom = document.getElementById(divId);
    if (!slotDom) {
      feAdConfig.warn('Abort Display: '+divId+' is not in DOM');
      return;
    }
    var slotTarget = slotDom.getAttribute('data-slot-name');
    if (!slotTarget) {
      feAdConfig.warn('Abort Display: '+divId+' has no data-slot-name attribute');
      return;
    }

    if ( defineAdSlot(divId) ) {
      googletag.cmd.push(function () {
        var slotObj = feAdSlotsConfig[slotTarget];
        if (!slotObj) {
          feAdConfig.warn('Abort Display: ' + slotTarget + ' does not map to an object');
          return;
        }
        if (!slotObj.defined) {
          feAdConfig.log('Abort Display: ' + slotTarget + ' was not defined');
          return;
        }
        if (slotObj.definedCount) {
          var slotIdx = parseInt(slotDom.getAttribute('data-slot-idx'), 10);
          if (slotIdx >= slotObj.definedCount) {
            feAdConfig.log('Abort Display: ' + slotTarget + ' only defined for up to ' + slotObj.definedCount + ' [idx=' + slotIdx + ']');
            return;
          }
        }

        feAdConfig.log('Display: ' + slotTarget + ' @ #' + divId);
        console.log("CALL: googletag.display on " + divId);
        googletag.display(divId);
      });
    }
  };

  /**
   * Build a map of all of the valid div IDs that can be associated with an ad slot
   *
   * @param adSlotKey string Name of the ad slot (e.g. '/21817035599/Mobile_Sticky_Footer')
   */
  var enumerateFeAdSlotDivIds = function(adSlotKey) {
    var definedDivIds = [];
    var slotObj = feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotKey];

    feAdConfig.decideDefineAd(adSlotKey, slotObj);

    if (!slotObj.defined) {
      feAdConfig.log('SKIP SLOT: ' + adSlotKey, slotObj.definedReason, slotObj.definedCount);
      return;
    }

    if (slotObj.definedCount) {
      for (var i = 0; i < slotObj.definedCount; i++) {
        var divId = slotObj.divId + '_' + i;
        definedDivIds.push(divId);
        feDivToAdSlots[divId] = adSlotKey;
      }
    } else {
      definedDivIds.push(slotObj.divId);
      feDivToAdSlots[slotObj.divId] = adSlotKey;
    }
    slotObj.definedDivIds = definedDivIds;
  };

  /**
   * Given a div ID figure out which ad unit it is to be associated with and set up that
   * association
   *
   * @param divId string The DIV we are placing an ad into (e.g. div-gpt-135143523423413-0_1)
   */
  var defineAdSlot = function(divId) {
    var adSlotKey = feDivToAdSlots[divId];
    var slotObj = feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotKey];

    if (!slotObj) {
      console.log("skipping define for " + divId + " / " + adSlotKey);
      return false;
    }

    googletag.cmd.push(function() {
      console.log("CALL: googletag.defineSlot for " + adSlotKey + " on " + divId, slotObj.sizes);

      var slot = googletag
        .defineSlot(adSlotKey, slotObj.sizes, divId);

      if ( slot ) {
        slot.addService(googletag.pubads());
        feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotKey].slots[divId] = slot;
        feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotKey].viewability[divId] = {
          viewableSince: null,
          timer: null,
          totalViewableTime: 0
        };

        if ( ENABLE_AMAZON ) {
          console.log("Defining A9 for " + adSlotKey + " on div " + divId);
          if (!window.apstagSlots) window.apstagSlots = [];
          window.apstagSlots.push({
            slotID: divId,
            sizes: feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotKey].sizes,
            slotName: adSlotKey
          });
        }
      }
    });

    return true;
  };

  function buildBids(slotObj, slotName) {
    var bids = [];

    if ( ENABLE_PREBID ) {
        if (slotObj.pbjsBid_districtM_placementId) {
            bids.push({
                bidder: 'districtm',
                params: {
                    placementId: slotObj.pbjsBid_districtM_placementId
                }
            });
        }

        if (slotObj.pbjsBid_districtMDMX_params) {
            bids.push({
                bidder: 'districtmDMX',
                params: slotObj.pbjsBid_districtMDMX_params
            });
        }

        if (slotObj.pbjsBid_appnexus_params) {
            bids.push({
                bidder: 'appnexus',
                params: slotObj.pbjsBid_appnexus_params
            });
        }

        if (slotObj.pbjsBid_rubicon_params) {
            bids.push({
                bidder: 'rubicon',
                params: slotObj.pbjsBid_rubicon_params
            });
        }

        if (slotObj.pbjsBid_ix_params) {
            slotObj.sizes.forEach(function (size) {
                bids.push({
                    bidder: 'ix',
                    params: {
                        siteId: slotObj.pbjsBid_ix_params.siteId,
                        size: size
                    }
                });
            });
        }

        if (slotObj.pbjsBid_sovrn_params) {
            slotObj.pbjsBid_sovrn_params.forEach(function (tagId) {
                bids.push({
                    bidder: 'sovrn',
                    params: {tagid: tagId}
                });
            });
        }

        if (slotObj.pbjsBid_openx_params) {
            bids.push({
                bidder: 'openx',
                params: {delDomain: 'thedrive-d.openx.net', unit: slotObj.pbjsBid_openx_params}
            });
        }

        if (slotObj.pbjsBid_kargo_params) {
            bids.push({bidder: 'kargo', params: slotObj.pbjsBid_kargo_params});
        }

        if ( ENABLE_RHYTHM_ONE ) {
            bids.push({bidder: 'rhythmone', params: {placementId: '83228'}});
        }

        if ( ENABLE_EMX ) {
            if (slotObj.pbjsBid_emx_params) {
                bids.push({
                    bidder: 'emx_digital',
                    params: {tagid: slotObj.pbjsBid_emx_params}
                });
            }
        }

        if ( ENABLE_CONVERSANT ) {
            bids.push({
                bidder: 'conversant',
                params: {
                    site_id: '200911',
                    secure: 1
                }
            });
        }

        if (slotObj.pbjsBid_sonobi_params) {
            bids.push({
                bidder: 'sonobi',
                params: {placement_id: slotObj.pbjsBid_sonobi_params}
            })
        }

        if (slotObj.pbjsBid_gumgum_params) {
            Object.keys(slotObj.pbjsBid_gumgum_params).forEach(function (size) {
                var placementId = slotObj.pbjsBid_gumgum_params[size];
                if (size === 'sticky') {
                    bids.push({bidder: 'gumgum', params: {inScreen: placementId}});
                } else {
                    bids.push({bidder: 'gumgum', params: {inSlot: placementId}});
                }
            });
        }

        if (slotObj.pbjsBid_onemobile_params) {
            slotObj.pbjsBid_onemobile_params.forEach(function (placement) {
                bids.push({
                    bidder: 'onemobile',
                    params: {dcn: placement['dcn'], pos: placement['pos'], ext: {}}
                });
            })
        }
    }

    return bids;
  }

  /**
   * Fetch a list of ad units to request bids on.
   *
   * @param onlyVisible Boolean. If true, only returns ad units that have been viewable for 30 seconds
   * @return {adunits: [{code: _, mediaTypes: { banner: { sizes: [[_, _]] } }, bids: __}], slots: [Slot]}
   */
  function getPbjsAdUnits(onlyVisible) {
    var adunits = [];
    var allSlots = [];

    Object.keys(feAdSlotsConfig).forEach(function(adSlotKey) {
      var slotObj = feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotKey];
      if (!slotObj || !slotObj.definedDivIds || slotObj.definedDivIds.length < 1) {
        console.log("No slot configuration found for " + adSlotKey);
        return;
      }

      var visibleDivs = [];

      if (onlyVisible) {
        var foundVisible = false;
        console.log("Checking visibility on " + adSlotKey, slotObj);
        slotObj.definedDivIds.forEach(function(definedDivId) {
          var totalVisibleTime = slotObj.viewability[definedDivId].totalViewableTime;
          if ( slotObj.viewability[definedDivId].viewableSince != null )
            totalVisibleTime += ((new Date()).getTime() - slotObj.viewability[definedDivId].viewableSince) / 1000;

          console.log("Total Visible Time For " + adSlotKey + " on " + definedDivId + ": " + totalVisibleTime);

          if (totalVisibleTime >= 30) {
            console.log("Adding " + adSlotKey + " on " + definedDivId + " to refresh queue");
            foundVisible = true;
            visibleDivs.push(definedDivId);
            /* Reset the counter */
            feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotKey].viewability[definedDivId] = {totalViewableTime: 0, viewableSince: null};
          }
        });
        if (!foundVisible) {
          return;
        }
      } else {
        slotObj.definedDivIds.forEach(function(definedDivId) {
          visibleDivs.push(definedDivId);
        });
      }

      var bids = buildBids(slotObj, adSlotKey);

      visibleDivs.forEach(function(visibleDivId) {
        var slot = slotObj.slots[visibleDivId];
        if ( slot ) {
          allSlots.push(slot);
          var adunit = {
            code: visibleDivId,
            mediaTypes: {
              banner: {
                sizes: slotObj.sizes
              }
            },
            bids: bids
          };
          adunits.push(adunit);
        }
      });
    });
    return {adunits: adunits, slots: allSlots};
  }

  function buildBidConfigForDiv(adSlotId, divId) {
    var slotObj = feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotId];
    if ( !slotObj ) {
      console.log("No ad slot found for " + adSlotId);
      return;
    }

    if ( !slotObj.slots[divId] ) {
      console.log("No matching div " + divId + " for ad slot " + adSlotId);
      return;
    }

    return {
      adunits: [{
        code: divId,
        mediaTypes: {
          banner: {
            sizes: slotObj.sizes
          }
        },
        bids: buildBids(slotObj, adSlotId)
      }],
      slots: [slotObj.slots[divId]]
    }
  }

  function prebidCallback(slots, isFirst) {
    googletag.cmd.push(function() {
      var refreshingFooter = false;
      pbjs.setConfig({priceGranularity: "high", enableSendAllBids: false});
      pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync();
      if ( ENABLE_AMAZON ) { window.apstag.setDisplayBids(); }
      feAdConfig.log('PBJS Init Ad Server - Refresh');
      console.log("Loading " + slots.length + " slots", slots);
      slots.forEach(function (slot) {
        slot.setTargeting("site", "thedrive.com");
        if ( adSlotTargets.aid ) {
          slot.setTargeting("article", adSlotTargets.aid );
        } else if ( adSlotTargets.ch ) {
          slot.setTargeting("article", adSlotTargets.ch );
        }

        if (
            (segment && segment.contentCmsCategory && segment.contentCmsCategory === 'The War Zone') ||
            window.location.pathname.match(/^\/the-war-zone/)
        ) {
          slot.setTargeting("site_section", "the-war-zone" );
        } else {
          slot.setTargeting("site_section", "other" );
        }

        var contentKeyword = "other";
        if ( segment && segment.contentCmsTerms ) {
            if (
                segment.contentCmsTerms.includes("fighter jets") ||
                segment.contentCmsTerms.includes("b-21") ||
                segment.contentCmsTerms.includes("f-35") ||
                segment.contentCmsTerms.includes("b61") ||
                segment.contentCmsTerms.includes("b-1b") ||
                segment.contentCmsTerms.includes("f-15") ||
                segment.contentCmsTerms.includes("f-15e") ||
                segment.contentCmsTerms.includes("mig-29") ||
                segment.contentCmsTerms.includes("mig 29") ||
                segment.contentCmsTerms.includes("cessna") ||
                segment.contentCmsTerms.includes("usaf") ||
                segment.contentCmsTerms.includes("airplanes") ||
                segment.contentCmsTerms.includes("bombers")
            ) {
                contentKeyword = "airplane";
            }
        }
        slot.setTargeting("content_keyword", contentKeyword);

        if (isFirst) {
          slot.setTargeting("refresh", "false");
        } else {
          slot.setTargeting("refresh", "true");
        }
        if ( slot.getAdUnitPath() === "/21817035599/Desktop_Tablet_Sticky_Footer"
          || slot.getAdUnitPath() === '/21817035599/Mobile_Sticky_Footer'
        ) {
          refreshingFooter = slot.getAdUnitPath();
        }
      });
      googletag.pubads().refresh(slots);

      if (refreshingFooter) {
        setTimeout(
          function() { refreshAd(refreshingFooter, feAdSlotsConfig[refreshingFooter].divId); },
          AD_REFRESH_TIME_SECONDS * 1000
        );
      }
    });
  }

  function refreshAd(adSlotId, divId) {
      if ( noRefreshAdUnits && noRefreshAdUnits.includes(divId) ) {
          console.log("Skipping refresh on ad unit with Direct campaign");
          return;
      }
    console.log("Refreshing a single ad: " + adSlotId + ", " + divId);
    if ( adSlotId.match("Desktop_Tablet_Sticky_Footer") && document.visibilityState && document.visibilityState !== 'visible' ) {
      console.log("Delaying sticky footer refresh until visible again");
      setTimeout(
        function() { refreshAd(adSlotId, divId); }, 5000
      );
    } else {
      pbjs.que.push(function () {
        var unitsAndDivs = buildBidConfigForDiv(adSlotId, divId);
        if (ENABLE_AMAZON) {
          window.apstag.fetchBids({
            slots: [{slotID: divId, sizes: feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotId].sizes, slotName: adSlotId}],
            timeout: PREBID_TIMEOUT
          });
        }
        pbjs.requestBids({
          adUnits: unitsAndDivs['adunits'],
          bidsBackHandler: function () {
            prebidCallback(unitsAndDivs['slots']);
          },
          timeout: PREBID_TIMEOUT
        });
      });
    }
  }

  window.__trackadm_usp_cookie = 'td-opt-out';
  window.getCookie = function(name) {
      var parts = ("; " + document.cookie).split("; " + name + "=");
      if (parts.length === 2) {
          return parts.pop().split(";").shift();
      } else {
          return null;
      }
  };

  /**
   * Replace any ccpa cmp functionality on page. The website will implement
   * the "do not collect" page and set a cookie. We read from that cookie
   * and implement the cmp api portion.
   */
  window.__uspapi = function(cmd, args, callback) {
      if (cmd === 'getUSPData') {
          /* Check for our consent cookie, return appropriate consent string
           * Full consent = '1YN-'
           * Opt-out = '1YY-'
           */
          if (getCookie(window.__trackadm_usp_cookie) === 'on') {
              /* The user has explicitly opted out */
              callback({'uspString': '1YY-'}, true);
          } else {
              /* Default case is opt-in */
              callback({'uspString': '1YN-'}, true);
          }
      }
  };
  </script>
  <script>
   /* Include Connatix On Test Page */
    if ( window.location.href.match(/20876/) ) {
        !function (n) {
            if (!window.cnxps) {
                window.cnxps = {}, window.cnxps.cmd = [];
                var t = n.createElement('iframe');
                t.display = 'none', t.onload = function () {
                    var n = t.contentWindow.document, c = n.createElement('script');
                    c.src = '//cd.connatix.com/connatix.playspace.js', c.setAttribute('async', '1'), c.setAttribute('type', 'text/javascript'), n.body.appendChild(c)
                }, n.head.appendChild(t)
            }
        }(document);
    }
  </script>

     <h2 class="featured-sections__bucket-title">
      <a href="topic/tech">
       Tech
      </a>
     </h2>
     <ul class="featured-bucket">
      <li class="featured-bucket__item--bucket">
       <a href="/tech/39829/gasoline-demand-may-have-already-peaked-thanks-to-the-pandemic">
        <figure class="featured-bucket__figure">
         <img alt="" class="featured-bucket__image" src="/content/2018/01/20180129-gas-station.jpg?quality=85&amp;width=712&amp;height=400&amp;quality=55"/>
        </figure>
       </a>
       <div class="featured-bucket__item-meta">
        <a href="/tech/39829/gasoline-demand-may-have-already-peaked-thanks-to-the-pandemic">
         <h3 class="featured-bucket__item-title">

        g = p.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
        g.parentNode.insertBefore(A, g)
    }("apstag", window, document, "script", "//c.amazon-adsystem.com/aax2/apstag.js");
    apstag.init({pubID: "49cdee1c-072d-4765-8313-7c45826cbedc", adServer: "googletag"});
    window.apstagSlots = [];
}

(function() {
    window.loadAds = function () {
        if (ENABLE_ADS) {
            Object.keys(feAdSlotsConfig).forEach(function (adSlotKey) {
                enumerateFeAdSlotDivIds(adSlotKey);
            });

            if (window.location.href.indexOf("/reviews") === -1 && !window.DISABLE_ADS) {
                addPrebidBelowPost();
                addPrebidFooter();
                addColumnSetAds();
                addArticleAds();
                addWideAd();
                addFeaturedArticleAds();
            }
            window.refreshBanLineItems = [
                193948414,
                193949566,
                193949356,
                193948420,
                5395493274,
                5396225929,
                5396225932,
                5396225935
            ];
            window.noRefreshAdUnits = [];

            pbjs.que.push(function () {
                googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                    var unitsAndDivs = getPbjsAdUnits(false);
                    pbjs.addAdUnits(unitsAndDivs['adunits']);
                    googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
                    googletag.enableServices();
                    googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function (event) {
                        /* Check event.lineItemId to see if its in refresh-ban list */
                        if (refreshBanLineItems.includes(event.slot.getSlotElementId())) {
                            if (!noRefreshAdUnits.includes(event.slot.getSlotElementId())) {
                                noRefreshAdUnits.push(event.slot.getSlotElementId());
                            }
                        }
                    });
                    googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotVisibilityChanged', function (event) {
                        var divId = event.slot.getSlotElementId();
                        /* Google puts _0, _1, etc on the ad slots when they are defined */
                        var adSlotId = event.slot.getSlotId().toString();
                        var inViewPercent = event.inViewPercentage;

                        // Handle special case of a close button that needs to be aligned to the div height
                        setTimeout(function() { refreshCloseButtonPosition(divId) }.bind(this), 1000);

                        console.log("Got SlotVisibilityChanged event for " + divId +
                            " with slot " + adSlotId + " percent " +
                            inViewPercent, event.slot);

                        adSlotId = adSlotId.substring(0, adSlotId.lastIndexOf("_"));

                        /* Skip the Sticky Footer which get refreshed every 30 seconds no matter what */
                        if (adSlotId === '/21817035599/Desktop_Tablet_Sticky_Footer' ||
                            adSlotId === '/21817035599/Mobile_Sticky_Footer'
                        ) {
                            console.log("Ignoring the Sticky Footer");
                            return;
                        }

                        var viewability = feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotId].viewability[divId];

                        /* If the ad has just started to be visible, start the timer */
                        if (inViewPercent >= 50 && viewability.viewableSince == null) {
                            feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotId].viewability[divId].viewableSince = (new Date()).getTime();
                            var totalVisible = feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotId].viewability[divId].totalViewableTime;
                            feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotId].viewability[divId].timer = setTimeout(function () {
                                feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotId].viewability[divId].viewableSince = null;
                                feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotId].viewability[divId].totalViewableTime = 0;
                                refreshAd(adSlotId, divId);
                            }, (AD_REFRESH_TIME_SECONDS - totalVisible) * 1000);
                        }
                        /* Otherwise if it is ceasing to be visible, add up it's history and cancel the timer */
                        else if (inViewPercent < 50 && viewability.viewableSince != null) {
                            var diffMillis = (new Date()).getTime() - feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotId].viewability[divId].viewableSince;
                            feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotId].viewability[divId].viewableSince = null;
                            clearTimeout(feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotId].viewability[divId].timer);
                            feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotId].viewability[divId].totalViewableTime += (diffMillis / 1000);
                            console.log("Total Accumulated Viewable Time for " + divId + " / " + adSlotId + " is " +
                                feAdSlotsConfig[adSlotId].viewability[divId].totalViewableTime + " seconds");
                        }
                    });
                    pbjs.bidderSettings = {
                        districtm: {
                            bidCpmAdjustment: function (bidCpm, bid) {
                                /* 85% Publisher/15% District M */
                                return bidCpm * 0.85;
                            }
                        },
                        rubicon: {
                            bidCpmAdjustment: function (bidCpm, bid) {
                                /* 80% Publisher/20% Rubicon */
                                return bidCpm * 0.80;
                            }
                        }
                    };
                    if (ENABLE_AMAZON) {
                        apstag.fetchBids({
                            slots: apstagSlots,
                            timeout: PREBID_TIMEOUT
                        });
                    }
                    console.log("CALL: pbjs.requestBids [root]");
                    pbjs.setConfig({priceGranularity: "high", enableSendAllBids: false});
                    pbjs.requestBids({
                        adUnits: unitsAndDivs['adunits'],
                        bidsBackHandler: function () {
                            prebidCallback(unitsAndDivs['slots'], true);
                        },
                        timeout: PREBID_TIMEOUT
                    });
                });
            });
        }

        function newElement(element, attributes) {
            var elem = document.createElement(element);
            Object.keys(attributes).forEach(function (key) {
                elem.setAttribute(key, attributes[key]);
            });
            return elem;
        }

        function addPrebidBelowPost() {
            var footers = document.getElementsByTagName("footer");
            if (footers.length > 0) {
                var adBelowPost = newElement("div", {
                    "id": 'div-gpt-ad-1558460740069-0',
                    "data-slot-name": '/21817035599/Desktop_Tablet_Below_Post',
                    "data-slot-target": 'desktopTablet'
                });
                footers[0].insertBefore(adBelowPost, footers[0].childNodes[0]);
                maybeDisplayFeAdSlot('div-gpt-ad-1558460740069-0');
            }
        }

        function addPrebidFooter() {
            var footers = document.getElementsByTagName("footer");
            if (footers.length > 0) {
                var mobileSticky = newElement("div", {
                    "id": 'div-gpt-ad-1558461864435-0',
                    "data-slot-name": '/21817035599/Mobile_Sticky_Footer',
                    "data-slot-target": 'mobile'
                });
                footers[0].appendChild(mobileSticky);
                addCloseButton(mobileSticky, footers[0], "mobile");

                maybeDisplayFeAdSlot('div-gpt-ad-1558461864435-0');

                var desktopSticky = newElement("div", {
                    "id": 'div-gpt-ad-1558461162727-0',
                    "data-slot-name": '/21817035599/Desktop_Tablet_Sticky_Footer',
                    "data-slot-target": 'desktopTablet'
                });
                footers[0].appendChild(desktopSticky);
                addCloseButton(desktopSticky, footers[0], "desktop");

                maybeDisplayFeAdSlot('div-gpt-ad-1558461162727-0');
            }
        }

        /**
         * Adapted from TrackADM: https://github.com/empireio/trackadm.com/blob/master/src/adm/templates/admin/ad-pixels/pixel.js.twig#L460
         */
        function addCloseButton(adDiv, wrapperDiv, postFix) {
          /* Ignore this if we aren't configured to show it */
          if ( !window.trackADMData || !window.trackADMData.closeButton ) {
            return;
          }

          var closeButton = document.createElement("div");
          closeButton.id = "trackadmFooterCloseBtn" + postFix;
          closeButton.innerText = "X";
          closeButton.style.position = "fixed";
          closeButton.style.display = "none";
          closeButton.style.right = "5px";
          closeButton.style.bottom = "90px";
          closeButton.style.zIndex = "100000";
          closeButton.style.cursor = "pointer";
          closeButton.style.width = "16px";
          closeButton.style.height = "16px";
          closeButton.style.border = "1px solid black";
          closeButton.style.fontWeight = "bold";
          closeButton.style.fontSize = "10px";
          closeButton.style.fontFamily = "Arial, sans-serif";
          closeButton.style.backgroundColor = "white";
          closeButton.style.textAlign = "center";
          closeButton.style.borderRadius = "15px";
          closeButton.style.paddingTop = "1px";
          closeButton.dataset.target = adDiv.id;

          adDiv.dataset.closeButton = closeButton.id;

          closeButton.onclick = function() {
            var element = document.getElementById(this.dataset.target);
            if ( element ) {
              element.remove();
              this.remove();
            }
          }

          wrapperDiv.appendChild(closeButton);
        }

        /**
         * Refreshes the vertical positioning of the footer close button.
         *
         * Adapted from TrackADM: https://github.com/empireio/trackadm.com/blob/master/src/adm/templates/admin/ad-pixels/pixel.js.twig#L853
         *
         * @param adUnitDivId
         */
        function refreshCloseButtonPosition(adUnitDivId) {
          /* Ignore this if we aren't configured to show it */
          if ( !window.trackADMData || !window.trackADMData.closeButton ) {
            return;
          }

          var div = document.getElementById(adUnitDivId);
          if ( div && div.dataset.closeButton ) {
            var closeButton = document.getElementById(div.dataset.closeButton);
            if ( closeButton ) {
              if ( div.offsetHeight ) {
                closeButton.style.bottom = (div.offsetHeight - 10) + "px";
                closeButton.style.display = "block";
              } else {
                closeButton.style.display = "none";
              }
            }
          }
        }

        function addArticleAds() {
            var numHPUnits = numHPUnits || 0;
            [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll('.feed-col-ad .ad div')).forEach(function (adNode, adIdx) {
                adNode.insertAdjacentHTML('afterend',
                    '<div class="drv-ad-slot" id="div-gpt-ad-1558461558608-0_' + adIdx + '"'
                    + '  data-slot-name="/21817035599/Desktop_Tablet_Sidebar_(Category//Home)"'
                    + '  data-slot-target="desktopTablet"'
                    + '  data-slot-idx="adIdx"'
                    + '></div>');
                maybeDisplayFeAdSlot("div-gpt-ad-1558461558608-0_" + adIdx);
                numHPUnits = numHPUnits + 1;
            });

            [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll('#article .has-ad-column .articleFragment')).forEach(function (adNode, adIdx) {
                if (adNode.insertAdjacentHTML) {
                    adNode.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend',
                        '<div><div class="drv-ad-slot" id="div-gpt-ad-1558460967123-0_' + adIdx + '"'
                        + '  data-slot-name="/21817035599/Desktop_Tablet_Content(Article)"'
                        + '  data-slot-target="desktopTablet"'
                        + '  data-slot-idx="adIdx"'
                        + '></div>'
                        + '<div class="drv-ad-slot" id="div-gpt-ad-1558461758503-0_0"'
                        + '  data-slot-name="/21817035599/Mobile_Content"'
                        + '  data-slot-target="mobile"'
                        + '  data-slot-idx="adIdx"'
                        + '></div></div>'
                    );
                    maybeDisplayFeAdSlot("div-gpt-ad-1558460967123-0_" + adIdx);
                    maybeDisplayFeAdSlot("div-gpt-ad-1558461758503-0_0");
                }
            });

            [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll('#article .ad[data-ad-type="teAd"], #article .ad[data-ad-type="mobileAd"]')).forEach(function (adNode, adIdx) {
                if (adNode.insertAdjacentHTML) {
                    adNode.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend',
                        '<div id="div-gpt-ad-1558461758503-0_' + (adIdx + 1) + '"'
                        + '  data-slot-name="/21817035599/Mobile_Content"'
                        + '  data-slot-target="mobile"'
                        + '  data-slot-idx="adIdx"'
                        + '></div>'
                    );
                    maybeDisplayFeAdSlot("div-gpt-ad-1558461758503-0_" + (adIdx + 1));
                }
            });
        }

        function addColumnSetAds() {
            var parents = [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll(".has-ad-column .ad-column"));
            var stickyCount = stickyCount || 0;
            if (parents.length) {
                var newsBody = document.getElementById("article");
                if (newsBody) {
                    newsBody.classList.add("article-with-ads");
                }
                parents.forEach(function (parent) {
                    var topAdParent = parent.querySelector(".ad");
                    if (topAdParent) {
                        var topAdDivId = 'div-gpt-ad-1558461470058-0_' + stickyCount;
                        topAdParent.appendChild(newElement("div", {
                            "id": topAdDivId,
                            "data-slot-name": '/21817035599/Desktop_Tablet_Top_Sidebar',
                            "data-slot-target": 'desktopTablet'
                        }));

                        maybeDisplayFeAdSlot(topAdDivId);
                    }

                    /* Make sure we have room for a 250px height + a 600px height ad */
                    if (parent.parentNode.offsetHeight > 860) {
                        var stickyAdDivId = 'div-gpt-ad-1558461667845-0_' + stickyCount;
                        var stickyWrapper = newElement("div", {
                            "class": 'ad sticky-ad',
                            "data-ad-type": 'coldAd'
                        });
                        stickyWrapper.appendChild(newElement("div", {
                            "id": stickyAdDivId,
                            "data-slot-name": '/21817035599/Desktop_Tablet_Sticky_Sidebar_(Article)',
                            "data-slot-target": 'desktopTablet'
                        }));
                        parent.appendChild(stickyWrapper);

                        maybeDisplayFeAdSlot(stickyAdDivId);
                    } else {
                        console.log("AD TECH - skipping Sticky Sidebar Slot. Height = " + parent.offsetHeight);
                        console.log(parent);
                    }

                    stickyCount = stickyCount + 1;
                });
            }
        }

        function addWideAd() {
            var parent = document.querySelector('.wide-ad');
            if (parent) {
                parent.appendChild(newElement("div", {
                    "id": 'div-gpt-ad-1558461406990-0',
                    "data-slot-name": '/21817035599/Desktop_Tablet_header',
                    "data-slot-target": 'desktopTablet'
                }));
                maybeDisplayFeAdSlot('div-gpt-ad-1558461406990-0');
            }
        }

        function addFeaturedArticleAds() {
            var elems = [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll(".wellAdWrapper .ad"));
            var count = 0;

            elems.forEach(function (parent) {
                var wellMobileAdDivId = 'div-gpt-ad-1558461758503-0_' + count;
                parent.appendChild(newElement("div", {
                    "id": wellMobileAdDivId,
                    "data-slot-name": '/21817035599/Mobile_Content',
                    "data-slot-target": 'mobile',
                    "data-slot-idx": count
                }));
                maybeDisplayFeAdSlot(wellMobileAdDivId);
                count++;
            });
        }
    }

    setTimeout(window.loadAds, window.__adDelay);
})();
  </script>
 </body>
</html>
